### Horror/Suspense Vlog Style Video Prompt: The Mirror Glitch

![‰∏≠Êñá](https://img.shields.io/badge/lang-‰∏≠Êñá-red)

> A detailed, multi-scene video generation prompt for Seedance 2.0 in a pseudo-documentary (Vlog) style, focusing on a suspenseful scenario where a mirror reflection exhibits independent, glitch-like behavior, requiring a reference image for the main character.

```
[Style] Pseudo-documentary (Vlog Style), hyperrealism, fixed camera shot feel, natural light, with a touch of suspense and horror. 
[Duration] 15 seconds 
[Protagonist (Remember to upload a reference image)] A sexy young woman preparing to wash up and sleep in front of the sink in her bathroom. 
[00:00-00:06] Scene 1: Normalcy. Setting: In front of a large ordinary bathroom mirror. Action: The protagonist is brushing her teeth, mouth full of foam. She makes various funny faces at the mirror while brushing (winking and grimacing). Key Detail: The reflection in the mirror is completely normal and synchronized. 
[00:06-00:11] Scene 2: The Glitch. Action: The protagonist finishes brushing, spits out the foam, and turns to leave the bathroom. High-Energy Moment (Core Climax): Just as the protagonist's real body has turned and left the mirror's frame, the ‚Äúreflection‚Äù in the mirror **does not move**! The ‚Äúreflection‚Äù remains in the brushing posture, even smirking and winking at the camera. It stays for a full 2 seconds before suddenly ‚Äúscreen-flashing‚Äù in panic to catch up with the body's movement and disappearing. Director's Note: Must create an extremely realistic ‚Äúnetwork latency‚Äù feel, giving the impression that the reflection has an independent consciousness. 
[00:11-00:15] Scene 3: The Punchline. Action: The protagonist, who has reached the door, seems to sense something is wrong and quickly turns back to look at the mirror. Result: The mirror has completely returned to normal, empty, only reflecting the opposite wall. The protagonist looks confused and scared, glances around the room, and shows a horrified expression. The scene freezes on the protagonist's bewildered face (horror movie effect).
```

<img src="https://customer-qs6wnyfuv0gcybzj.cloudflarestream.com/9ede32e6df9aeab295b6eeb17e56ae07/thumbnails/thumbnail.jpg" width="600" alt="Horror/Suspense Vlog Style Video Prompt: The Mirror Glitch">

### Cinematic Prompt for Boxers Sparring Comparison

![English](https://img.shields.io/badge/lang-English-blue)

> A detailed cinematic prompt used to compare Kling 3.0 and Seedance 2.0 outputs, focusing on a handheld shot of two boxers practice sparring in a gritty gym, emphasizing realism, camera movement, and character stability.

```
Handheld shot circling two boxers practice sparring in a gritty gym, purposefully missing each other with their swings. Sweat droplets, sharp impacts, breathing intensity. Shallow depth of field, practical lighting, visceral realism, stable identity. Duration: 10s. Aspect ratio: 16:9. Photoreal cinematic. Single shot unless specified. Avoid text, captions, watermarks, logos. Stress camera movement: smooth parallax, consistent objects, stable faces; no text
```

### Absurd Reversal: Politician Ignored for Steamed Buns

![‰∏≠Êñá](https://img.shields.io/badge/lang-‰∏≠Êñá-red)

> A detailed, multi-scene video prompt for Seedance 2.0, featuring a high-stakes political scene that takes an absurd, humorous turn when the enthusiastic crowd ignores the main character to rush a steamed bun shop. The prompt specifies locations, character actions, camera movements, and atmosphere for each of the four scenes.

```
Scene 1: Horse Galloping + Enthusiastic Crowd Approaching (0:00-0:08, 8 seconds)
‚Ä¢ Location: Main winding road in a Vancouver mansion district (wide asphalt road, large detached mansions on both sides, evergreen pine trees covered with light snow)
‚Ä¢ Subject: A rider in a dark suit galloping at full speed on a white horse, the horse's four hooves airborne, mane flying
‚Ä¢ Environment: Light snow falling, mansions flashing past, outline of the North Shore mountains and ocean in the distance
‚Ä¢ Crowd: A large group of enthusiastic supporters suddenly appears ahead (diverse young people), waving yellow dragon flags + ‚ÄúNothing‚Äù signs, shouting and cheering, surging towards the rider
‚Ä¢ Camera: Front medium-speed follow-shot ‚Üí Switch to the rider's perspective (POV), the crowd getting closer
‚Ä¢ Atmosphere: Climax continues, the rider has a confident smile, preparing to rein in (hand already raised to the reins, relaxed posture, corners of the mouth turned up)
Scene 2: Reversal‚ÄîThe crowd passes directly through, ignoring the rider (0:08-0:14, 6 seconds)
‚Ä¢ Location: Same road, a Chinese steamed bun shop appears at the corner (sign ‚ÄúQingfeng Baozi Shop‚Äù, warm lighting, simple plastic tables and chairs in the outdoor seating area, steam rising)
‚Ä¢ Subject: The rider is about to wave in greeting, but the crowd ignores him, rushing past him on both sides/around him, heading for the queue/entering the bun shop entrance
‚Ä¢ Action: The rider's smile freezes, his hand stops mid-air, his expression changes from anticipation to shock/disarray (wind messes up his hair, the hem of his suit jacket flutters)
‚Ä¢ Details: The crowd shouts ‚ÄúBaozi! Baozi!‚Äù, yellow dragon flags wave chaotically, the ‚ÄúNothing‚Äù sign is pushed aside; the white horse is forced to take small steps or turn aside to avoid the crowd
‚Ä¢ Camera: Quick pan/wide shot, showing the crowd flowing like a tide around the rider (the horse is ‚Äúpassed through‚Äù in the center of the frame), the rider is left alone in the middle
‚Ä¢ Atmosphere: Absurd reversal, awkward disarray, black humor climax
Scene 3: Eating buns and dialogue outside the bun shop (0:14-0:20, 6 seconds)
‚Ä¢ Location: Qingfeng Baozi Shop outdoor seating area (plastic tables and chairs, steaming baskets, mansion district road in the background)
‚Ä¢ Subject: Two ordinary young people (wearing down jackets) sitting in the queue seats, eating buns heartily
‚Ä¢ Action: One person takes a bite of a bun, closes their eyes in satisfaction, ‚ÄúAh, so delicious.‚Äù (Close-up shot of the bun being bitten open, showing steam/juice)
‚Ä¢ Dialogue:

First person (eating while looking towards the road): Who is that?
Second person (thoughtfully, chewing the bun, looking into the distance): Nothing.
‚Ä¢ Camera: Medium shot of two people ‚Üí Slight push-in on facial expressions (satisfied + calm), the faint silhouette of the rider walking away is visible in the background
‚Ä¢ Atmosphere: Down-to-earth, contrasting cuteness, referencing the theme ‚Äúnothing‚Äù

Scene 4: The rider laughs at himself, continues on his way (0:20-0:30, 10 seconds)
‚Ä¢ Location: Wide, extending road in the mansion district (straight ahead, the mansion cluster gradually receding)
‚Ä¢ Subject: The rider on the horse, his expression changing from disarray to a confident smile
‚Ä¢ Action: He reaches into his suit chest pocket, pulls out a packaged sandwich, takes a big bite (juice/crumbs splatter), then shakes his head with a dashing smile, lightly taps the white horse with the reins, and continues galloping forward
‚Ä¢ Environment: The mansion cluster gradually shrinks in the background, the evergreen trees on both sides of the road and the supporters (now stopped) can only be seen waving from afar, the Vancouver-style mountain-sea skyline in the distance (misty with snow)
‚Ä¢ Details: The white horse's tail swings, hoof prints are left on the lightly snow-covered road, the bite mark on the sandwich is clear, the rider smiles confidently
‚Ä¢ Camera: From close-up (sandwich bite special shot) ‚Üí Slowly pulls back to an extreme long shot, low-angle shooting, emphasizing the ‚ÄúI don't care‚Äù isolated heroic feeling; finally fades out.
```

<img src="https://customer-qs6wnyfuv0gcybzj.cloudflarestream.com/93f4fd2f550ea1b830b1e46182538ac9/thumbnails/thumbnail.jpg" width="600" alt="Absurd Reversal: Politician Ignored for Steamed Buns">

**‰ΩúËÄÖ:** [John](https://x.com/john87445528) | **‰æÜÊ∫ê:** [Link](https://x.com/john87445528/status/2021706240272069021) | **ÁôºÂ∏ÉÊôÇÈñì:** Feb 12, 2026

### Surreal Battlefield Ronin Action Scene Prompt

![English](https://img.shields.io/badge/lang-English-blue)

> A highly detailed creative description for an action scene featuring a masked ronin battling a colossal winged beast on floating rock islands in a thunderstorm, specifying camera movements, effects, and the dramatic finale.

```
A surreal battlefield in the sky: floating rock islands drifting through a thunderstorm, clouds swirling below like an ocean. The masked ronin dashes across the drifting platforms, pursued by a colossal winged beast whose chest is a swirling vortex of storm clouds and lightning. The camera hurtles from island to island, struggling to keep up as rocks tilt, spin, and crumble away beneath them. Every wingbeat sends shockwaves through the air, shaking the frame and blowing debris and rain straight into the viewer‚Äôs face. Rapid handheld cuts capture the ronin leaping impossible gaps, sword carving arcs of light that briefly cut through the darkness. The finale shows the camera diving behind him as he jumps off the last crumbling rock, riding a bolt of lightning directly into the monster‚Äôs chest vortex with a final, all-or-nothing slash that explodes the storm from within and clears the sky in a blinding flash.
```

### Director's Prompt: The Flash Speed Sequence

![English](https://img.shields.io/badge/lang-English-blue)

> A detailed, multi-part 'Director's Prompt' for Seedance 2.0 via ChatCut, describing a cinematic sequence featuring The Flash accelerating, with specific camera angles, visual effects (lightning, motion blur), and scene transitions (city, highway, portal formation).

```
Opening Shot:
Extreme close-up on The Flash‚Äôs boots touching wet asphalt at night. Raindrops freeze midair as time slows. Golden lightning begins to crawl over his suit, crackling softly.
Camera: Low-angle, slow push-in.
As he leans forward, the world stretches and distorts. On the beat, he launches. The camera snaps into pursuit as he explodes forward in a blinding burst of red and gold lightning, tearing through the city streets. Buildings smear into light trails, traffic lights become streaks of color, thunder rolling underneath the sound design.

DIRECTOR‚ÄôS PROMPT ‚Äî PART 2

The Flash accelerates beyond the city, racing across highways, deserts, and oceans in seconds. The curvature of the Earth becomes visible as clouds rip apart beneath him.
Camera: Dynamic tracking shot with heavy motion blur, lightning arcing outward like veins of energy.
Time fractures ‚Äî day and night collapse into one continuous run. As he reaches maximum velocity, the lightning intensifies into near-white brilliance. He vanishes in a final thunderous flash, leaving only scorched air, fading electricity, and silence.

DIRECTOR‚ÄôS PROMPT ‚Äî PART 3

A low, resonant hum builds. The air ahead fractures like glass. A circular portal forms ‚Äî ancient, unstable ‚Äî glowing with swirling light and dust, as if time itself is being torn open.
```

### Live-Action Anime Adaptation: Water vs. Thunder Breathing

![‰∏≠Êñá](https://img.shields.io/badge/lang-‰∏≠Êñá-red)

> A highly detailed, three-scene video prompt for Seedance 2.0, generating a 15-second, high-octane battle between two characters using 'Water Breathing' (blue water dragon) and 'Thunder Breathing' (golden lightning) techniques, inspired by anime but rendered in a Hollywood live-action style.

```
Live-Action Anime Adaptation ¬∑ Breathing Technique Decisive Battle (15 seconds ¬∑ Super Burning Special Effects Version)
„ÄêCore Focus„Äë: Water Breathing (Blue Water Dragon) VS Thunder Breathing (Golden Lightning), live-action high-speed duel.

„ÄêStyle„Äë: Hollywood live-action anime movie texture, dark samurai style, 4K ultra-clear, extreme fast cuts, explosive particle light effects, no gore.
„ÄêDuration„Äë: 15 seconds
„ÄêScene„Äë: Misty forest under the moonlight, muddy ground, scattered falling leaves.

[00:00-00:05] Shot 1: Water Melody Prelude (Sense of Power Accumulation)
Visuals: A young samurai in a green and black checkered haori (jacket) lowers his center of gravity under the moonlight, gripping his sword with both hands.
Action: He takes a deep breath, and the surrounding air instantly solidifies. As he draws his sword, a huge blue water dragon, condensed from high-pressure water flow, appears out of thin air, rotating rapidly around his body and blade, emitting the roar of flowing water.
Special Effects Details: The water flow has a realistic sense of splashing water, illuminating the dark forest.

[00:05-00:10] Shot 2: Thunder Flash ¬∑ Charge (Sense of Extreme Speed)
Visuals: The opponent, a blonde swordsman wearing a yellow triangle-patterned haori, is crouched extremely low, adopting the posture of an Iaijutsu (sword drawing technique).
Action: The ground suddenly explodes, and he instantly transforms into a dazzling golden lightning afterimage, rapidly refracting and charging through the forest in a 'Z' shape at a speed undetectable by the naked eye.
Special Effects Details: Golden electric arcs and scorched fallen leaves remain in the air where he passed.

[00:10-00:15] Shot 3: Water and Thunder Collision ¬∑ Final Note (Ultimate Move Clash)
Visuals: Extreme speed confrontation. The young samurai swings the massive blue water dragon down to meet the charge, and the blonde swordsman, transformed into lightning, crashes into it head-on.
Action: The two swords violently collide at the center of the frame.
Special Effects Spectacle: The blue water dragon and the golden lightning instantly explode, forming a massive water-thunder energy storm that spreads outward. The surrounding trees are snapped in half by the energy wave, and mud and light obscure the camera. The scene ends in an intensely dazzling blue, yellow, and white light.
```

<img src="https://customer-qs6wnyfuv0gcybzj.cloudflarestream.com/2ecc3f47355480376c26b34eed07bbdd/thumbnails/thumbnail.jpg" width="600" alt="Live-Action Anime Adaptation: Water vs. Thunder Breathing">

**‰ΩúËÄÖ:** [John](https://x.com/johnAGI168) | **‰æÜÊ∫ê:** [Link](https://x.com/johnAGI168/status/2021610292979876208) | **ÁôºÂ∏ÉÊôÇÈñì:** Feb 11, 2026

Chinese Xianxia animation film style, ultra-fine 3D CG rendering, 15-second high-energy duel scene, strong contrast with gold and cyan dual color tones. 0-3 seconds: Extreme long shot, two streams of light rapidly collide from both sides of the screen in chaotic void‚Äîin the golden light on the left, a middle-aged cultivator in a greenish-gray robe is vaguely visible, his face calm like water, holding a small green sword, this is Han Li; in the cyan-black malevolence on the right, a thin man with white hair and a black robe stands with his hands behind his back, his eyes deep like ancient wells, surrounded by world-destroying aura, this is Wang Lin. Seventy-two flying swords transform into a golden storm of sword rain sweeping forward; Wang Lin points with his right hand, and a massive cyan giant hand illusion that covers the sky condenses behind him. The giant hand slaps down against the sword rain. The moment the sword energy and palm force collide, a golden and cyan energy torrent erupts. The shockwave spreads in all directions, tearing the void, accompanied by the sound of metal collision and space shattering. 9-12 seconds: Freeze-frame slow motion. A golden illusion of ten thousand Buddhas appears behind Han Li, his eyes burst with golden light, and Ten Thousand Swords Return to One condenses into a hundred-zhang golden sword light that strikes straight down; a hint of madness flashes in Wang Lin's eyes, and he roars, "If heaven does not tolerate me, I will defy this heaven!". He raises his right hand high, and a spinning black sphere condenses in his palm, emitting a destructive aura that warps space. The two ultimate forces collide head-on, and time seems to stand still. 13-15 seconds: Massive energy explosion. The screen is swallowed by white light and slowly dissipates. In the dust, two figures stand back-to-back in the shattered void, their robes tattered, both gasping for breath. Han Li speaks faintly, "I admire your heaven-defying technique, Fellow Daoist Wang." A smile appears at the corner of Wang Lin's mouth. The sound effects fade into the crisp sound of void fragments falling and a weakening wind.

![‰∏≠Êñá](https://img.shields.io/badge/lang-‰∏≠Êñá-red)

„ÄêFilm Settings„ÄëCinematic quality, IMAX aspect ratio, ARRI Alexa 65mm, high contrast, cyberpunk aesthetic, 8K resolution.

„ÄêCore Concept„ÄëSpace-time folding. A transformation from an ancient, pure Salt Lake Goddess instantly awakening into a neon warrior of the future city.

Shot 3: Jump cut, glitch art interference. The screen is instantly torn apart by intense neon light. The white salt lake background instantly transforms into a flashing holographic billboard of a cyber city on a rainy night.

Shot 4: Medium shot, low-angle upward shot. Visual impact. She still stands in the center of the frame, but her ethnic robe has transformed into high-tech reflective functional clothing. The original silver headpiece has become metallic, flowing headphones.

Shot 5: Close-up, light and shadow shifting. Rain falls on her face, reflecting pink and purple neon lights. She gives a cold smile to the camera, reaches out to put on goggles, and her aura is fully unleashed.

Shot 6: Extreme Long Shot, freeze frame. She stands atop a skyscraper, overlooking the entire steel jungle, with a giant holographic projection of a whale swimming behind her. Subtitle: ‚ÄúAwakening ¬∑ Future‚Äù.

Duration: 10 seconds | Style: Top Hollywood commercial film | Visual Impact: Extremely strong
```

### Urban Fantasy Short Drama: Good Luck Descends

![‰∏≠Êñá](https://img.shields.io/badge/lang-‰∏≠Êñá-red)

> A detailed, six-shot storyboard prompt for Seedance 2.0, designed for a vertical screen short drama in an urban fantasy style. The plot involves an anxious office worker (male lead) who is rescued by a tall, glowing 'Goddess of Luck' (female lead), transforming his stressful environment into a beautiful aurora and cloudscape.

```
Prompt Type: Short Drama Storyboard/Video Generation

Aspect Ratio: 9:16 (Vertical Screen)

Visual Style: Urban Fantasy, transition from reality to illusion, high definition, cinematic lighting, particle effects, healing aesthetic.

„ÄêCharacter Settings„Äë

Male Lead: Wearing a dark blue suit, initially anxious expression, average height, representing the ‚Äúworker‚Äù of the real world.

Female Lead: Wearing a white T-shirt and shorts, extremely tall, with braided pigtails, radiating a soft white halo all over, representing the ‚ÄúGoddess of Luck‚Äù from a higher dimension.

„ÄêPlot Storyboard and Dialogue„Äë

Shot 1: Medium Shot.

Content: The male lead stands in a gloomy office, holding a stack of reports, frowning, looking stressed. The surrounding air is also gray and hazy.

Subtitle/Dialogue: ‚ÄúThis project is too hard, who can save me...‚Äù

Shot 2: Close-up transitioning to Wide Shot.

Content: A beam of warm light suddenly hits next to the male lead. The camera pulls up to show the female lead's extremely tall figure. She appears out of nowhere, as if stepping out of a comic book, with a brilliant smile.

Subtitle/Dialogue: ‚ÄúI heard someone was making a wish?‚Äù

Shot 3: Two-person Medium Shot, height difference interaction.

Content: The male lead looks up in surprise (must convey this adorable looking-up feeling). The female lead bends down slightly and gently taps the documents in the male lead's hand.

Visual Effects: Golden magical particles explode where the fingertip touches.

Shot 4: Scene Change (Fantasy Moment).

Content: As the golden particles spread, the originally dull office background instantly disappears, turning into a spectacular aurora and sea of clouds. The male lead's suit becomes brand new and sharp, his expression changes from anxiety to surprise.

Subtitle/Dialogue: ‚ÄúFrom now on, I've got your luck covered.‚Äù

Shot 5: Close-up, eye contact.

Content: The two look at each other against the cloudscape background. The female lead winks playfully, the male lead scratches his head shyly.

Atmosphere: The scene is filled with pink and gold bubbles, extremely beautiful.

Shot 6: Freeze Frame Ending.

Content: The backs of the two standing side-by-side, facing a dazzling future city night view.

Subtitle Effect: Large text displaying ‚ÄúGood Luck Descends.‚Äù
```

### Cinematic Scene Prompt: Horseback Chase in a Luxury Estate

![‰∏≠Êñá](https://img.shields.io/badge/lang-‰∏≠Êñá-red)

> A detailed, multi-scene prompt for Seedance 2.0 to generate a dramatic, high-speed video sequence featuring a figure on a white horse galloping through a luxury Vancouver West Side estate, followed by a crowd of supporters, emphasizing strong visual impact and motion blur.

```
Scene 1: Galloping in front of the mansion gate (0:00-0:05, 5 seconds)
‚Ä¢ Location: In front of the main entrance of a top luxury mansion in Vancouver West Side (large estate-style villa, stone/wood structure gate, wide driveway entrance, surrounded by evergreen hedges)
‚Ä¢ Subject: A figure in a dark suit riding a horse galloping out of the mansion gate
‚Ä¢ Horse Action: White horse with all four hooves off the ground, mane flying, charging out at a fast pace or trot
‚Ä¢ Environment: Winter, light snow kicked up by the horse's hooves, mansion architecture clearly visible (large floor-to-ceiling windows, wood and stone combination, multi-story terrace), distant North Shore mountains or ocean outline faintly visible, evergreen pines covered with light snow
‚Ä¢ Crowd: Supporters on both sides dodge and make way while waving yellow dragon flags (blue dragon pattern + Hinomaru element) and cheering, holding white 'Nothing' signs
‚Ä¢ Camera: Frontal shot, white horse charging directly at the camera, strong sense of motion (slight low angle to enhance impact)
‚Ä¢ Atmosphere: Sharp entrance, unstoppable momentum, a stunning debut in a high-end private community

Scene 2: Crowd chasing close-up (0:05-0:09, 4 seconds)
‚Ä¢ Location: Next to a private winding road shaded by trees in the mansion area
‚Ä¢ Subject: A group of supporters running after the horse (mostly young people, wearing winter down jackets/coats)
‚Ä¢ Action: Running while raising hands, shouting, and pumping fists, trying to keep up with the horse's speed; some almost fall but continue the excited chase
‚Ä¢ Signage: Yellow dragon flags + white 'Nothing' signs are held up while running (signs shaking)
‚Ä¢ Background: Mansion exterior walls and evergreen pines quickly blur past, light snow mist or tree shadows blur and shake, distant mountains sweep past
‚Ä¢ Camera: Follow-up close-up, slight camera shake to create a sense of urgency and speed (handheld style or quick push/pull)
‚Ä¢ Atmosphere: Frenzied chase, urgent and excited, enthusiastic response from community residents
Scene 3: Galloping across the side of the mansion (0:09-0:15, 6 seconds)
‚Ä¢ Location: Side landscape driveway or lawn extension area of the mansion (side view shows large terrace, poolside or garden, evergreen hedges)
‚Ä¢ Subject: The figure on the white horse crosses the frame at a full gallop
‚Ä¢ Horse Action: Full speed running, the moment all four hooves are off the ground is clearly visible, tail flying like a flag, snow is kicked up
‚Ä¢ Environment: The side of the mansion quickly blurs past (wood and stone walls, multi-story windows blurred), adjacent mansion and evergreen forest on the left, background mountain/sea skyline sweeps past
‚Ä¢ Crowd: Supporters behind holding 'Nothing' signs + yellow dragon flags chase but gradually fall behind, some stop to wave and shout
‚Ä¢ Camera: High-speed side follow-shot, motion blur enhances the sense of speed (horse sweeps across the frame, background blurred)
‚Ä¢ Atmosphere: Lightning fast, unstoppable, a heroic gallop through a luxurious community
```

### Cinematic Aerial Wingsuit Flight Prompt

![English](https://img.shields.io/badge/lang-English-blue)

> An extremely detailed, cinematic prompt for an aerial video sequence, starting with a wide shot of a snow-covered mountain peak and transitioning into a high-speed, proximity wingsuit flight through ice formations and a glacial valley.

```
A cinematic video sequence opening with a serene wide aerial shot of a pristine snow-covered mountain peak at dawn, the summit piercing through a sea of clouds with alpenglow painting the ice formations pink and gold. The camera transitions to follow a wingsuit pilot who leaps from the peak, immediately entering a steep vertical dive through wispy clouds. The tracking shot positions just behind and above the pilot as they accelerate downward, the camera shaking subtly from air turbulence, frost particles streaming past. The pilot pulls into a proximity flight, skimming within meters of sheer cliff faces and jagged ice formations, the camera banking and rolling to match every precise movement. Shadows and light play across the wingsuit's surface as the pilot threads through a narrow ice chimney, walls rushing past in a blur of blue and white. Speed intensifies as they enter a massive glacial valley, weaving between enormous ice pillars and frozen waterfalls, mist and powder snow kicked up in spiraling trails. The pilot executes a dramatic barrel roll around a freestanding ice spire before pulling the parachute at the last possible moment. The camera follows upward through the deceleration, then pulls wide to reveal a breathtaking hidden alpine lake surrounded by untouched snow fields, perfectly still and mirror-like, reflecting the morning sky.
```

### Seedance 2.0 Prompting Techniques and Templates

![‰∏≠Êñá](https://img.shields.io/badge/lang-‰∏≠Êñá-red)

> A comprehensive guide to writing effective Seedance 2.0 prompts, including a universal formula (Subject + Action + Scene + Lighting + Camera Language + Style + Quality + Constraints), tips for describing actions and camera movements, stabilization techniques, and two ready-to-use templates for portrait and landscape videos.

```
‚ë† Universal Formula

Subject + Action + Scene + Lighting + Camera Language + Style + Quality + Constraints

Example:
A young girl walking slowly by the sea, hair gently moved by the breeze, natural smile, warm light at sunset, medium shot, slow push-in, stable and smooth footage, 4K high definition, cinematic feel, clear face without deformation.

‚ë° Action Description

Don't just write: walking / dancing
Write: slow + continuous + natural

Priority words:
slow, gentle, natural, continuous, smooth, not stiff

Useful combinations:
slow turn / gently raise hand / slightly lower head / sway with the wind

‚ë¢ Camera Language

Seedance is very strong at recognizing camera movements, remember to write:

Close-up / Medium Shot / Special Shot
Slow push-in / slight pull-out / smooth horizontal pan / stable follow-shot

Example:
Medium shot, slow push-in, stable follow-shot, smooth footage without stuttering

‚ë£ Anti-face change / Anti-deformation

Very important:

Clear face, stable features, no deformation
Normal human structure, natural proportions
Same character, consistent clothing, unchanged hairstyle

‚ë§ General words for quality enhancement

4K, ultra-high definition, rich details, sharp clarity
Cinematic feel, soft light and shadow, natural colors
No blur, no flicker, stable footage

‚ë• Style / Atmosphere words

Healing and fresh / Japanese style / Korean atmosphere
Retro film grain / dreamy soft light / cyberpunk
Minimalist clean / high-end texture

‚ë¶ Multi-shot writing (Advanced usage)

Describe in sequence, do not break up randomly:

Start with close-up of face ‚Üí slow pull-out ‚Üí character walks slowly ‚Üí camera follows smoothly ‚Üí end with a freeze-frame smile

‚ëß Avoidance Guide

‚ùå Intense running/jumping / complex multi-person interaction
‚ùå Vague words: good-looking / very beautiful / very cool
‚ùå Contradictory requirements: ultra-high speed + extreme stability

‚ë® Templates that can be copied directly

Portrait atmosphere short video
A young girl walking slowly in the forest, hair gently moved by the breeze, natural smile, medium shot, slow push-in, stable and smooth footage, 4K high definition, cinematic feel, clear face without deformation.

Landscape atmosphere
Sunset by the sea, waves gently lapping the beach, camera slowly panning horizontally, warm orange tones, smooth footage, 4K ultra-high definition, no flicker or ghosting.

‚ë© Summary of Tips

1Ô∏è‚É£ Write actions slowly and continuously
2Ô∏è‚É£ Write camera movements stably and simply
3Ô∏è‚É£ Must add stable / no deformation / not stiff
4Ô∏è‚É£ Quality & style are added last
5Ô∏è‚É£ Less complexity, more precision
```

<img src="https://customer-qs6wnyfuv0gcybzj.cloudflarestream.com/63668df8df46ae69a07bf1f8414b6ea1/thumbnails/thumbnail.jpg" width="600" alt="Seedance 2.0 Prompting Techniques and Templates">

**‰ΩúËÄÖ:** [web3Â•∂Á≥ñ](https://x.com/web3naitang) | **‰æÜÊ∫ê:** [Link](https://x.com/web3naitang/status/2021510580440608905) | **ÁôºÂ∏ÉÊôÇÈñì:** Feb 11, 2026

**[üé¨ ËßÄÁúãË¶ñÈ†ª ‚Üí](https://youmind.com/zh-TW/seedance-2-0-prompts?id=200)**

### Three-Shot Hostage Crisis Action Scene Prompt

![English](https://img.shields.io/badge/lang-English-blue)

> A detailed multi-shot prompt for a text-to-video test in Seedance 2.0, outlining a dramatic hostage crisis scenario involving a SWAT officer and a killer, specifying camera angles, dialogue, and technical style (high-shutter speed, handheld camera shake, 24fps).

```
[Shot 1: Frontal Menacing Shot] A medium shot of a SWAT officer in full tactical gear, gas mask, and helmet. He is pointing his assault rifle directly at the camera lens (breaking the fourth wall). He is shouting with visible intensity: "LET THE HOSTAGE GO! DROP THE WEAPON NOW!" [Shot 2: The Threat] Cut to a medium shot of the killer in a dirty tank top, holding a woman in a chokehold. He has a pistol pressed to her head. He is sweating and manic, screaming at the off-screen officer: "STAY BACK! I'LL KILL HER! I SWEAR I'LL DO IT!" [Shot 3: Over-the-Shoulder Resolution] The camera is positioned directly behind the SWAT officer's right shoulder. We see the back of his helmet and his rifle in the foreground. In the distance (mid-ground), the killer is still visible holding the girl. The killer screams one last time: "I'M GONNA DO IT!" after The officer's rifle kicks back with a single sho and hit head enemy. The killer falls instantly. The girl is left standing, shocked but safe. Technical Style: High-shutter speed action, realistic muzzle flashes, handheld camera shake, 24fps, English dialogue.
```

### Sun Wukong vs. Goku: Cross-Style Dimensional Clash

![‰∏≠Êñá](https://img.shields.io/badge/lang-‰∏≠Êñá-red)

> A complex, multi-scene video prompt for Seedance 2.0 (Jimen/Xiaoyunque) detailing a 15-second cross-style battle between the classic Chinese mythological Sun Wukong and the Japanese anime character Super Saiyan Goku. The prompt specifies the visual contrast, dialogue, special effects (Kamehameha, Ruyi Jingu Bang), and the final scene where the two styles merge into a new world.

```
15-second cross-style duel shot, with a sharp contrast between the Japanese anime cel-style on the left and the Chinese mythological realistic style on the right. 0-3 seconds: Extreme long shot, a dimensional rift descends from the center of the frame, splitting the scene in two‚Äîon the left is the red rocky wasteland typical of Dragon Ball, with Super Saiyan Goku in golden hair standing with one hand on his hip, his orange battle suit tightly defining his muscle lines, surrounded by the golden Super Saiyan electric aura; on the right is the cloud-shrouded Flower and Fruit Mountain, with the classical Sun Wukong in chain mail, phoenix-winged purple-gold helmet, and holding the Ruyi Jingu Bang, standing on the mountain peak, surrounded by auspicious clouds. The two look at each other across the rift, the edge of the rift flickers unstably due to the style conflict, accompanied by a low sound of spacetime distortion. 4-8 seconds: Both speak simultaneously‚ÄîAnime Goku: "You look a lot like me, buddy!" with a hot-blooded anime boy voice; Classical Wukong: "Bold demon monkey, how dare you steal my name!" with a deep operatic voice. The two rush out of the rift and cross paths. Anime Goku unleashes a Kamehameha wave of pink-blue energy, and Classical Wukong swings the Jingu Bang in a sweeping strike. The moment the energy wave and the Jingu Bang collide, a style-tearing effect occurs‚Äîthe intersection of the two forces pixelates and flickers, color blocks collapse and reorganize, accompanied by the angry roar of the Kamehameha "Ka-me-ha-me-HA" and the whistling sound of the Jingu Bang cutting through the air. 9-12 seconds: Freeze-frame slow motion. Anime Goku activates Ultra Instinct, his body shrouded in silver-gray aura, his eyes turning calm silver-gray, his movements flashing like lightning as he appears behind Classical Wukong; Classical Wukong's Fiery Eyes and Golden Pupils suddenly light up with golden-red light, his body transforms into an afterimage using the Dharma Heaven and Earth technique‚Äîhis body swells to a hundred zhang (hundreds of feet) tall, and the Jingu Bang in his hand simultaneously enlarges like a pillar supporting the sky, smashing down. 13-15 seconds: The lightning-fast punches of the silver-gray aura and the sky-high Jingu Bang collide head-on in the center of the frame. The shockwave tears the dimensional rift, and the Dragon Ball wasteland and Flower and Fruit Mountain are simultaneously swallowed by the energy torrent. After a flash of white light, the smoke and dust clear, and two figures stand back-to-back in the merged new world‚Äîa strange terrain mixing mountains and wasteland. Anime Goku scratches his head and laughs, saying, "That was some powerful stuff, let's fight again next time." Classical Wukong lightly strokes his monkey whiskers and nods, "I'll find another place to play next time." The sound effects converge into the hearty laughter of the two simultaneously and the fading sound of the wind.
```

```
„ÄêStyle„ÄëClassic Wuxia Film - [Ink Remnants of the Bamboo Forest], High-speed Cinematography, combination of live-action and CG, strong visual impact, fast pace, using ‚Äúcold tones‚Äù to enhance the depth of the bamboo forest. „ÄêDuration„Äë15 seconds „ÄêCharacters„ÄëA swordswoman in a fiery red dress, movements as light as a swallow, sharp sword energy. Dust flies up from the ground, the camera follows the movement. Eye contact, tense atmosphere, detail depiction. „Äê00:11 - 00:14„ÄëShot 6, Wide to CU, „ÄêAction„ÄëThe two pass each other, standing back-to-back. The camera switches to a close-up, a strand of severed hair slowly floats down in the air. Artistic conception, severed hair, elegant conclusion, slow motion.

### Northeast China MC Livestream Cyberpunk Prompt

![‰∏≠Êñá](https://img.shields.io/badge/lang-‰∏≠Êñá-red)

> A detailed, multi-shot prompt for Seedance 2.0 to generate a vertical-screen (9:16) video in the style of a high-end, cyberpunk-neon livestream studio, featuring a 'Northeast Sweet Girl' MC performing a slow-roll dance, accompanied by two cool bodyguards. The prompt specifies the visual style, music, character details, and shot breakdown for a highly rhythmic and glamorous atmosphere.

```
„ÄêStyle„ÄëDouyin/Kuaishou vertical screen (TikTok Portrait 9:16), high-end influencer livestream studio (High-end Livestream Studio), cyberpunk neon light, 4K quality, Northeast MC Slow Roll style (Dongbei MC Slow Roll), extremely strong sense of rhythm.
„ÄêDuration„Äë15 seconds
„ÄêBGM Setting„Äë‚ÄúNight Paris‚Äù DJ Slow Roll version.
„ÄêCharacters„Äë
1. Protagonist: Northeast Sweet Girl, extremely sweet and cute appearance (twin pigtails/big eyes), but dressed in a ‚Äúsweet and cool style‚Äù (pink fuzzy jacket + tight camisole), wearing huge rhinestone headphones, holding a professional condenser microphone.
2. Supporting Roles: Two black-clad subordinates (Backups), wearing sunglasses, expressionless, standing on the left and right sides behind the sweet girl, cool like bodyguards.

[00:00-00:05] Shot 1: Sweet Girl Starts the Vibe (The Intro).
Visuals: Lights focus on the sweet girl's face. She smiles sweetly at the camera, then her eyes instantly become sharp (entering MC state).
Action: Following the heavy bass rhythm of ‚Äúboom-chick-a-boom‚Äù, she presses one hand against her headphones and starts swaying rhythmically left and right (Swaying).
Background: The two black-clad subordinates behind her synchronously start nodding and shaking their shoulders, movements perfectly aligned, creating a strong sense of pressure.
„ÄêAtmosphere„ÄëHigh-end, hazy, decadent.

[00:05-00:10] Shot 2: Night Paris Climax (The Climax).
Visuals: The large screen in the background of the livestream studio displays brilliant neon words ‚ÄúNight Paris‚Äù and a laser projection of the Eiffel Tower.
Action: The sweet girl holds the microphone with both hands, looking intoxicated and confident, swaying significantly with the rhythm. The two subordinates behind her cooperate by performing the ‚Äúhand flower‚Äù gesture, maximizing the atmosphere.
„ÄêVisual Details„ÄëGolden streamers and champagne-colored light spots float in the air, and the lights flash wildly with the rhythm.

[00:10-00:15] Shot 3: Full Display (The Finale).
Visuals: The camera pulls back slightly to show the entire luxurious livestream studio.
Action: The sweet girl makes an extremely cool ‚Äúgun shooting‚Äù gesture (Wink) at the camera. The two subordinates behind her simultaneously pull out their sunglasses, put them on straight, and then cross their arms, looking incredibly cool.
„ÄêEffects„ÄëThe screen is filled with virtual gift effects (sports cars, yachts) exploding around the sweet girl, and the frame freezes on the trio's coolest pose.
```

### Anime Mech Battle Prompt

### High-Octane Tollywood Action Scene Prompt

![‰∏≠Êñá](https://img.shields.io/badge/lang-‰∏≠Êñá-red)

> A detailed, multi-shot prompt for Seedance 2.0 to generate a high-energy action scene in the style of an Indian Tollywood blockbuster. The scene features a confident hero defying physics, using palm wind to launch enemies, and kicking a jeep into the air, emphasizing exaggerated slow-motion, anti-gravity effects, and intense visual impact.

```
„ÄêStyle„Äë
Indian Telugu action blockbuster (Tollywood Action Blockbuster), extremely exaggerated physics effects (Anti-gravity Physics), slow-motion ramping and fast/slow cuts (Ramp-mo), dust flying, epic BGM atmosphere, no gore, focus on impact.

„ÄêDuration„Äë15 seconds

„ÄêScene„Äë
A dusty abandoned quarry or construction site, strong sunlight, very windy.

„ÄêCharacters„Äë
Protagonist (Hero): With a signature beard, wearing sunglasses, a denim jacket, walking with a swagger, extremely confident and dominant expression.
Opponents (Goons): Dozens of thugs in messy clothes, whose main purpose is to be knocked flying.

„ÄêShot Breakdown„Äë
[00:00-00:05] Shot 1: Divine Entrance and Minions Taking Flight (The Hero Entry)
Visuals: Extreme slow motion (Super Slow-mo). The protagonist walks slowly, with a sky full of yellow sand whipped up by the strong wind behind him.
Action: He casually raises his hand and waves (looks effortless).
Spectacular Effect: Just the force of his palm wind causes the five thugs rushing at the front to fly high backward like broken kites, defying the laws of physics (at least 15 meters high), spinning in slow motion in the air.

[00:05-00:10] Shot 2: Newton's Laws Fail (Physics Defied)
Visuals: Fast/slow cut switching. The protagonist instantly accelerates and rushes into the crowd.
Action: The protagonist executes a spinning kick. The target hit instantly knocks down ten people behind him, creating a domino effect.
Spectacular Effect: A huge shockwave causes a circle of dust to explode from the ground. All thugs, upon contact with the protagonist's fists and feet, are dramatically ejected outwards, accompanied by large amounts of white dust (replacing blood), smashing surrounding wooden crates and props.

[00:10-00:15] Shot 3: The Ultimate Power Move
Visuals: The protagonist takes off his sunglasses and gives a wicked smile at the camera (Blinking Moment).
Action: A jeep rushes towards him. He neither dodges nor avoids it, kicking it directly with his foot.
Spectacular Effect: The moment the jeep touches his toe, it is vertically kicked high into the air like a toy car, tumbling and scattering parts. The protagonist calmly puts his sunglasses back on and adjusts his hair against the backdrop of falling car parts and flying thugs.
```

<img src="https://customer-qs6wnyfuv0gcybzj.cloudflarestream.com/801bc927d2c0952197a7e0e9024e4dd8/thumbnails/thumbnail.jpg" width="600" alt="High-Octane Tollywood Action Scene Prompt">

### Cinematic Horror Tracking Shot Prompt

![English](https://img.shields.io/badge/lang-English-blue)

> A highly detailed, multi-part prompt for a cinematic horror scene involving a medium tracking shot down a corridor, specific sound effects, camera jolts, and a creature collision, emphasizing cinematic horror realism.

```
Medium tracking shot following a character walking quickly down a corridor from behind.The camera follows at shoulder height, steady and close.AMBIENCE: distant ventilation noise, subtle rumble.The character slows down slightly, sensing something wrong.SFX: faint whisper-like sound moving from left to right in the stereo space.Without warning, a creature slams violently out of a side doorway, colliding with the character and throwing them sideways against the wall.SFX: explosive impact, bone-crushing hit, sudden creature scream.The camera jolts slightly from the shock but does not cut.The creature pins the character briefly, snarling close to their face.BGM: aggressive low-frequency hit, then sustained dread tone.Chaotic motion, strong physicality, cinematic horror realism.
```

### Gothic Cathedral Battle: Dragon vs. Warriors

![‰∏≠Êñá](https://img.shields.io/badge/lang-‰∏≠Êñá-red)

> A highly detailed, multi-scene video prompt for Seedance 2.0, describing a 15-second fast-paced battle against a black dragon in the ruins of a Gothic cathedral. The prompt specifies the actions of two warriors (spear-wielding female, shield-bearing male), camera movements (shake, follow, pan), and the final explosive confrontation.

```
Create a battle using the three characters and scene in the image. „ÄêScene Setting„Äë Gothic cathedral ruins, collapsed stone pillars, twilight filtering through broken stained glass, dust floating. 0-3 seconds: The female warrior advances cautiously with a spear, the camera follows her back. Suddenly, a black dragon pounces from the shadows, sharp claws tear the ground flagstones, debris explodes. The female warrior rolls and dodges, the spear draws an arc of light. The camera shakes violently, the dragon's roar echoes through the cathedral. 4-6 seconds: The black-armored warrior rushes in, his shield slams the side of the dragon's head, a dull roar of metal hitting bone. The dragon's head is knocked aside, saliva sprays from its sharp teeth. Quick cut to the female warrior, she leaps up, the spear tip stabs directly into the gap between the scales on the dragon's neck, sparks fly. The camera follows the moment of spear impact. 7-9 seconds: The black dragon angrily sweeps its tail, the tail blade cuts through a stone pillar. The pillar collapses with a crash, falling towards the two warriors. The black-armored warrior holds up his shield to resist the impact, the shield surface dents, his feet plow deep marks in the ground. The female warrior slides low, passing through the rain of debris, her spear scraping sparks on the ground. The dragon's wings spread, obscuring the light, plunging the cathedral into shadow. 10-12 seconds: The female warrior fiercely stabs the dragon's abdomen, the spear shaft sinking deep. The black dragon painfully throws its head back and roars, its neck swelling, a red glow surging in its throat. The black-armored warrior senses danger, charges and tackles the female warrior, rolling her backward. The next instant, dragon fire erupts, a column of flame engulfs the spot where they were moments ago, the flagstones melting into lava. The camera distorts in the heatwave. 13-15 seconds: Both warriors launch their finishing moves simultaneously. The black-armored warrior shield-bashes the dragon's neck joint from the flank, and the female warrior throws her spear with full force from the front, the shaft spinning as it penetrates the dragon's throat. The black dragon's body stiffens, crashing heavily onto the ground, kicking up a cloud of dust. The camera pulls back and freezes: the two warriors stand panting, the giant dragon lies dead in the center of the cathedral, the twilight filtering through the broken stained glass illuminating the battlefield ruins. Quick fade to black. Ôøº „ÄêStyle Description„Äë ‚Ä¢ Fast-paced editing, no slow motion ‚Ä¢ Camera shakes violently upon impact, dust explosion ‚Ä¢ Close-up special shots capturing the moment weapons collide with scales ‚Ä¢ Maintain a dark Gothic atmosphere throughout, firelight and twilight interwoven ‚Ä¢ Sound effects: metal clashing, dragon roar, pillar collapse, fire roaring „ÄêCamera Movement„Äë Follow-shot push-in ‚Üí Shaking close-up ‚Üí Horizontal pan sweep ‚Üí Heatwave distortion ‚Üí Pull-out freeze frame
```

<img src="https://customer-qs6wnyfuv0gcybzj.cloudflarestream.com/2bc632f6de6aca79609ef134cc9054a2/thumbnails/thumbnail.jpg" width="600" alt="Gothic Cathedral Battle: Dragon vs. Warriors">

**‰ΩúËÄÖ:** [John](https://x.com/john87445528) | **‰æÜÊ∫ê:** [Link](https://x.com/john87445528/status/2021391303259431011) | **ÁôºÂ∏ÉÊôÇÈñì:** Feb 11, 2026

**[üé¨ ËßÄÁúãË¶ñÈ†ª ‚Üí](https://youmind.com/zh-TW/seedance-2-0-prompts?id=191)**
